*Shiyuan Zhang,Qiwei Di,Xuheng Li,Quanquan Gu*

Main category: cs.LG

Relevance: 15.0

TL;DR: 本文证明了离散化欠阻尼朗之万动力学（ULD）在KL散度上的首个维度无关收敛界，改进了之前维度依赖的结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有离散化ULD的收敛保证通常随维度d多项式增长，在高维情况下变得无意义。虽然已有Wasserstein-2距离的维度无关结果，但KL散度的维度无关保证一直缺失。

Method: 将KL局部误差框架（Altschuler et al., 2025）精化到维度无关设置，得到依赖于Hessian上界矩阵迹tr(H)而非维度d的界。

Result: 获得了离散化ULD的首个维度无关KL散度界，在tr(H)≪d的情况下，欠阻尼朗之万蒙特卡洛相对于过阻尼方法有改进的迭代复杂度。

Conclusion: 填补了离散化ULD在KL散度维度无关收敛理论上的空白，为高维采样提供了更实用的理论保证。

Abstract: Underdamped Langevin dynamics (ULD) is a widely-used sampler for Gibbs distributions $π\propto e^{-V}$, and is often empirically effective in high dimensions. However, existing non-asymptotic convergence guarantees for discretized ULD typically scale polynomially with the ambient dimension $d$, leading to vacuous bounds when $d$ is large. The main known dimension-free result concerns the randomized midpoint discretization in Wasserstein-2 distance (Liu et al.,2023), while dimension-independent guarantees for ULD discretizations in KL divergence have remained open. We close this gap by proving the first dimension-free KL divergence bounds for discretized ULD. Our analysis refines the KL local error framework (Altschuler et al., 2025) to a dimension-free setting and yields bounds that depend on $\mathrm{tr}(\mathbf{H})$, where $\mathbf{H}$ upper bounds the Hessian of $V$, rather than on $d$. As a consequence, we obtain improved iteration complexity for underdamped Langevin Monte Carlo relative to overdamped Langevin methods in regimes where $\mathrm{tr}(\mathbf{H})\ll d$.

</details>


### [409] [The power of small initialization in noisy low-tubal-rank tensor recovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02729)
*ZHiyu Liu,Haobo Geng,Xudong Wang,Yandong Tang,Zhi Han,Yao Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

Relevance: 15.0

TL;DR: 该论文研究张量恢复问题，针对带噪声线性测量下的低管秩张量恢复，提出使用小初始化策略的因子梯度下降方法，解决了过参数化时恢复误差随过估计管秩线性增长的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在张量恢复问题中，当使用因子梯度下降（FGD）方法时，如果过估计管秩R（即R>实际管秩r），在密集噪声（如高斯噪声）存在的情况下，传统的光谱初始化会导致恢复误差随过估计的管秩R线性增长。这在实际应用中是一个严重问题，因为真实管秩r通常是未知的。

Method: 提出使用小初始化策略的因子梯度下降方法。将优化变量分解为U*U^⊤形式，其中U∈ℝ^{n×R×k}，然后应用因子梯度下降。通过四阶段分析框架，理论证明小初始化可以使FGD达到近似极小极大最优的恢复误差，即使管秩R被显著过估计。同时提出易于使用的早停策略。

Result: 理论分析表明，小初始化策略使FGD的恢复误差与过估计的管秩R无关，达到了当前已知的最尖锐误差界。早停策略在实践中也能达到最佳效果。这些理论结果通过模拟实验和真实数据实验得到验证。

Conclusion: 该研究解决了张量恢复中过参数化带来的误差增长问题，通过小初始化策略使因子梯度下降方法对管秩过估计具有鲁棒性，为张量恢复提供了更实用的解决方案。

Abstract: We study the problem of recovering a low-tubal-rank tensor $\mathcal{X}\_\star\in \mathbb{R}^{n \times n \times k}$ from noisy linear measurements under the t-product framework. A widely adopted strategy involves factorizing the optimization variable as $\mathcal{U} * \mathcal{U}^\top$, where $\mathcal{U} \in \mathbb{R}^{n \times R \times k}$, followed by applying factorized gradient descent (FGD) to solve the resulting optimization problem. Since the tubal-rank $r$ of the underlying tensor $\mathcal{X}_\star$ is typically unknown, this method often assumes $r < R \le n$, a regime known as over-parameterization. However, when the measurements are corrupted by some dense noise (e.g., Gaussian noise), FGD with the commonly used spectral initialization yields a recovery error that grows linearly with the over-estimated tubal-rank $R$. To address this issue, we show that using a small initialization enables FGD to achieve a nearly minimax optimal recovery error, even when the tubal-rank $R$ is significantly overestimated. Using a four-stage analytic framework, we analyze this phenomenon and establish the sharpest known error bound to date, which is independent of the overestimated tubal-rank $R$. Furthermore, we provide a theoretical guarantee showing that an easy-to-use early stopping strategy can achieve the best known result in practice. All these theoretical findings are validated through a series of simulations and real-data experiments.

</details>

Abstract: The shock response spectrum (SRS) is widely used to characterize the response of single-degree-of-freedom (SDOF) systems to transient accelerations. Once trained, the model generates signals consistent with prescribed target spectra without requiring iterative optimization. These results establish deep generative modeling as a scalable and efficient approach for inverse SRS reconstruction.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We investigate geometric regularization strategies for learned latent representations in encoder--decoder reduced-order models. Across multiple seeds, we find that (a)--(c) often produce latent representations that make subsequent latent-dynamics training with a frozen autoencoder more difficult, especially for long-horizon rollouts, even when they improve local decoder smoothness or related sensitivity proxies. In contrast, (d) consistently improves conditioning-related diagnostics of the learned latent dynamics and tends to yield better rollout performance. We discuss the hypothesis that, in this setting, the downstream impact of latent-geometry mismatch outweighs the benefits of improved decoder smoothness.

### [416] [From Reachability to Learnability: Geometric Design Principles for Quantum Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03071)
*Vishal S. Ngairangbam,Michael Spannowsky*

Main category: quant-ph

Relevance: 15.0

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一个量子神经网络(QNN)的几何学习框架，通过引入CLA映射和aCLS准则，证明QNN需要数据和可训练权重的联合依赖才能实现几何灵活性，而不仅仅是状态可达性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典深度网络通过深度实现数据表示的几何变形，但量子神经网络中深度或状态可达性本身并不能保证这种特征学习能力。作者旨在理解QNN中几何特征学习的本质条件。

Method: 在纯态设置下，将编码数据视为$\mathbb{C}P^{2^n-1}$中的嵌入流形，通过李代数方向分析无穷小酉作用。引入Classical-to-Lie-algebra (CLA)映射和almost Complete Local Selectivity (aCLS)准则，该准则结合了方向完备性和数据依赖的局部选择性。

Result: 证明数据无关的可训练酉算子是完备但非选择性的（可学习的刚性重定向），而纯数据编码是选择性但不可调的（固定变形）。几何灵活性需要数据和可训练权重的非平凡联合依赖。多量子比特状态流形的高维变形需要参数化的纠缠方向，固定纠缠器如CNOT无法提供自适应几何控制。

Conclusion: QNN设计应从状态可达性重新框架为隐藏量子表示的可控几何。满足CLS的数据重新上传模型在仅需四分之一门操作的情况下优于不可调方案。

Abstract: Classical deep networks are effective because depth enables adaptive geometric deformation of data representations. In quantum neural networks (QNNs), however, depth or state reachability alone does not guarantee this feature-learning capability. We study this question in the pure-state setting by viewing encoded data as an embedded manifold in $\mathbb{C}P^{2^n-1}$ and analysing infinitesimal unitary actions through Lie-algebra directions. We introduce Classical-to-Lie-algebra (CLA) maps and the criterion of almost Complete Local Selectivity (aCLS), which combines directional completeness with data-dependent local selectivity. Within this framework, we show that data-independent trainable unitaries are complete but non-selective, i.e. learnable rigid reorientations, whereas pure data encodings are selective but non-tunable, i.e. fixed deformations. Hence, geometric flexibility requires a non-trivial joint dependence on data and trainable weights. We further show that accessing high-dimensional deformations of many-qubit state manifolds requires parametrised entangling directions; fixed entanglers such as CNOT alone do not provide adaptive geometric control. Numerical examples validate that CLS-satisfying data re-uploading models outperform non-tunable schemes while requiring only a quarter of the gate operations. Thus, the resulting picture reframes QNN design from state reachability to controllable geometry of hidden quantum representations.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管已有广泛研究，但由于理论和计算限制，准确表征一般非线性系统的吸引域（DOA）仍然具有挑战性，特别是在存在不确定性和状态约束的情况下。需要开发能够处理这些复杂性的新方法。

Method: 1. 在紧致集度量空间中引入新的值函数来表征DOA；2. 建立其基本数学性质并推导相关的Bellman型（Zubov型）泛函方程；3. 开发物理信息神经网络（PINN）框架，通过将Bellman型方程直接嵌入训练过程来学习相应的值函数；4. 引入验证程序，利用现有形式验证工具从学习的神经网络近似中获得可证明的安全鲁棒DOA估计。

Result: 该方法在四个涉及受状态约束的非线性不确定系统的数值示例中证明了其有效性和适用性，并与文献中的现有方法进行了性能比较。

Conclusion: 该论文提出了一种新颖的框架，能够准确估计具有状态约束和不确定性的离散时间非线性系统的安全鲁棒吸引域，通过结合理论分析、神经网络学习和形式验证，为解决这一具有挑战性的问题提供了有效的解决方案。

Abstract: Analyzing nonlinear systems with attracting robust invariant sets (RISs) requires estimating their domains of attraction (DOAs). Despite extensive research, accurately characterizing DOAs for general nonlinear systems remains challenging due to both theoretical and computational limitations, particularly in the presence of uncertainties and state constraints. In this paper, we propose a novel framework for the accurate estimation of safe (state-constrained) and robust DOAs for discrete-time nonlinear uncertain systems with continuous dynamics, open safe sets, compact disturbance sets, and uniformly locally $\ell_p$-stable compact RISs. The notion of uniform $\ell_p$ stability is quite general and encompasses, as special cases, uniform exponential and polynomial stability. The DOAs are characterized via newly introduced value functions defined on metric spaces of compact sets. We establish their fundamental mathematical properties and derive the associated Bellman-type (Zubov-type) functional equations. Building on this characterization, we develop a physics-informed neural network (NN) framework to learn the corresponding value functions by embedding the derived Bellman-type equations directly into the training process. To obtain certifiable estimates of the safe robust DOAs from the learned neural approximations, we further introduce a verification procedure that leverages existing formal verification tools. The effectiveness and applicability of the proposed methodology are demonstrated through four numerical examples involving nonlinear uncertain systems subject to state constraints, and its performance is compared with existing methods from the literature.

</details>


### [418] [The elbow statistic: Multiscale clustering statistical significance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03235)
*Francisco J. Perez-Reche*

Main category: stat.ML

Relevance: 15.0

TL;DR: ElbowSig将启发式的"肘部方法"形式化为严格的统计推断问题，通过聚类异质性序列的归一化离散曲率统计量，评估多分辨率聚类结构，提供算法无关的聚类数量选择框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有聚类数量选择标准通常只针对单一"最优"划分，忽略了数据中可能存在的多分辨率统计显著结构。需要一种能够识别多尺度组织结构的正式统计推断方法。

Method: 基于聚类异质性序列的归一化离散曲率统计量，在无结构数据的零分布下进行评估。推导了该统计量在大样本和高维情况下的渐近性质，兼容硬聚类、模糊聚类和基于模型的聚类等多种方法。

Result: 在合成和实证数据集上的广泛实验表明，该方法能够控制I型错误率，同时具备识别多尺度组织结构的能力，这些结构通常被单分辨率选择标准所掩盖。

Conclusion: ElbowSig提供了一个算法无关的统计框架，能够正式识别数据中的多分辨率聚类结构，解决了传统方法只关注单一最优划分的局限性。

Abstract: Selecting the number of clusters remains a fundamental challenge in unsupervised learning. Existing criteria typically target a single ``optimal'' partition, often overlooking statistically meaningful structure present at multiple resolutions. We introduce ElbowSig, a framework that formalizes the heuristic ``elbow'' method as a rigorous inferential problem. Our approach centers on a normalized discrete curvature statistic derived from the cluster heterogeneity sequence, which is evaluated against a null distribution of unstructured data. We derive the asymptotic properties of this null statistic in both large-sample and high-dimensional regimes, characterizing its baseline behavior and stochastic variability. As an algorithm-agnostic procedure, ElbowSig requires only the heterogeneity sequence and is compatible with a wide range of clustering methods, including hard, fuzzy, and model-based clustering. Extensive experiments on synthetic and empirical datasets demonstrate that the method maintains appropriate Type-I error control while providing the power to resolve multiscale organizational structures that are typically obscured by single-resolution selection criteria.

</details>


### [419] [Gravity Falls: A Comparative Analysis of Domain-Generation Algorithm (DGA) Detection Methods for Mobile Device Spearphishing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03270)
*Adam Dorian Wong,John D. Hastings*

Main category: cs.CR

Relevance: 15.0

TL;DR: 该论文评估了传统和机器学习DGA检测器在smishing（短信钓鱼）场景下的性能，发现现有方法对不断演变的DGA战术适应能力有限


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前DGA研究主要关注恶意软件C2和电子邮件钓鱼数据集，缺乏对smishing驱动的DGA域检测的评估，特别是针对移动设备威胁的研究

Method: 使用Gravity Falls半合成数据集（2022-2025年smishing链接），评估两种字符串分析方法（香农熵和Exp0se）和两种ML检测器（LSTM分类器和COSSAS DGAD），以Top-1M域名作为良性基线

Result: 检测性能高度依赖DGA战术：对随机字符串域性能最高，但对字典拼接和主题组合抢注变体性能下降，多个工具/集群配对的召回率较低

Conclusion: 传统启发式方法和近期ML检测器都不适合Gravity Falls中观察到的持续演变的DGA战术，需要更上下文感知的方法，并为未来评估提供可复现基准

Abstract: Mobile devices are frequent targets of eCrime threat actors through SMS spearphishing (smishing) links that leverage Domain Generation Algorithms (DGA) to rotate hostile infrastructure. Despite this, DGA research and evaluation largely emphasize malware C2 and email phishing datasets, leaving limited evidence on how well detectors generalize to smishing-driven domain tactics outside enterprise perimeters. This work addresses that gap by evaluating traditional and machine-learning DGA detectors against Gravity Falls, a new semi-synthetic dataset derived from smishing links delivered between 2022 and 2025. Gravity Falls captures a single threat actor's evolution across four technique clusters, shifting from short randomized strings to dictionary concatenation and themed combo-squatting variants used for credential theft and fee/fine fraud. Two string-analysis approaches (Shannon entropy and Exp0se) and two ML-based detectors (an LSTM classifier and COSSAS DGAD) are assessed using Top-1M domains as benign baselines. Results are strongly tactic-dependent: performance is highest on randomized-string domains but drops on dictionary concatenation and themed combo-squatting, with low recall across multiple tool/cluster pairings. Overall, both traditional heuristics and recent ML detectors are ill-suited for consistently evolving DGA tactics observed in Gravity Falls, motivating more context-aware approaches and providing a reproducible benchmark for future evaluation.

</details>


### [420] [Optimizing Orbital Parameters of Satellites for a Global Quantum Network](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02480)
*Athul Ashok,Owen DePoint,Jackson MacDonald,Albert Williams,Don Towsley*

Main category: quant-ph

Relevance: 5.0

TL;DR: 该论文研究量子卫星星座设计，使用贝叶斯优化和遗传算法优化卫星轨道参数，以最大化全球地面站之间的纠缠生成率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 由于地面量子链路的根本限制，卫星作为全球量子互联网的纠缠生成源受到广泛关注。需要设计优化的卫星星座来最大化全球分布式地面站之间的纠缠生成率。

Method: 采用两种黑盒优化框架：贝叶斯优化（BO）和遗传算法（GA），优化卫星倾角和卫星集群分配，以实现对固定全球地面站的最大纠缠生成率。

Result: 两种方法都取得了可比较的结果，表明它们对此优化任务的有效性。BO通常收敛更高效，而GA在后期表现出更好的增长，表明对局部最大值的不敏感性较低。两种方法相比仅考虑地面站覆盖的朴素方法都有显著改进。

Conclusion: 贝叶斯优化和遗传算法都是设计量子卫星星座的有效方法，能够显著提升全球量子网络的纠缠生成性能。

Abstract: Due to fundamental limitations on terrestrial quantum links, satellites have received considerable attention for their potential as entanglement generation sources in a global quantum internet. In this work, we focus on the problem of designing a constellation of satellites for such a quantum network. We find satellite inclination angles and satellite cluster allocations to achieve maximal entanglement generation rates to fixed sets of globally distributed ground stations. Exploring two black-box optimization frameworks: a Bayesian Optimization (BO) approach and a Genetic Algorithm (GA) approach, we find comparable results, indicating their effectiveness for this optimization task. While GA and BO often perform remarkably similar, BO often converges more efficiently, while later growth noted in GAs is indicative of less susceptibility towards local maxima. In either case, they offer substantial improvements over naive approaches that maximize coverage with respect to ground station placement.

</details>
